msg:First of all, I admit that the surrounding environment of this hotel is really good on sunny days, with mountains, water, fields and scenery. But I personally think that these are the scenery outside the hotel, thanks to nature, not the hotel itself.

The points are for natural scenery, and then there are a lot of complaints about this trip! Three days and two nights, almost two nights + two noons without sleep! Therefore, the first thing I did when I got up on the third day was to leave quickly, which was really uncomfortable! Therefore, I will definitely not give a good review! !

The biggest complaint: hotel facilities and services! !
1. Facilities and equipment:
About air conditioning: There are few buttons, and the cold and hot switching is not smart. For three days, the children and adults were sweating in the room every day! I called the front desk on the first day and said that they adjusted it? No one came. I called again on the second day, and someone came. It was lonely and it was still hot when I slept! Cooling and heating in the middle of the night! This air conditioner is really a failure! The indoor temperature of 23‚ÑÉ is almost the same as 30‚ÑÉ.

About parent-child facilities and equipment: In fact, many people have given points that the hotel needs to improve in online reviews, but I still haven't seen it! For example, the indoor children's playground is small and messy, unmanaged, and a mess! There is only a small mini play area outdoors, and another area has three or two slides that are also charged... I really can't complain about this so-called outdoor facility! I really don't understand what this is? I don't recommend parent-child travel with too high expectations. It's okay to climb the mountain and see the reservoir, but forget about the children's play.

About the guest room facilities: On the first day, there were combs in the room, no toothbrush sets, and they were sent after feedback. But I found that the toothbrush sets for children were not sent on the second day without saying anything? There are no men's razors in the guest room. You say this is a business hotel, it doesn't have this thing, you say it is for environmental protection, they promote disposable cotton shoes. You say he saves money, how much is this thing worth?

About the hotel's peripheral facilities, as the comrades in the comment area unanimously agree, there is no stool to stand on, it is hot and depressing, the grass can hardly be sat on after rain, and the facilities are very imperfect!

2. Service:
I didn't want to comment, but I really couldn't bear it anymore! Although the feedback can be solved in the first time, they are always on the road to remedy and keep making mistakes. It's really speechless! This service is really a flaw! 

About the experience of the doorman of the hotel that claims to be "five-star": the car arrived at the door, it was raining! We saw someone at the door, but no one came. Well, we got off the car and asked how to check in and how to park! After checking in, the suitcases that helped to push were returned to us directly. There was no sense of service, even though we didn't need help to send it upstairs. Well, that's it. 

About the cleaning of the guest room: the biggest depressing point this time! At 2 o'clock in the afternoon, we were sleeping and resting. Because we didn't lock the door, the cleaning lady knocked on the door and pushed the door in! My husband woke up from his dream and ran out to tell her to speak softly and not come in to clean for the time being. Who knew that the other party actually screamed directly? ! Completely ignoring whether we were resting? Shouldn't we scream? ! The child woke up directly! Speechless! The explanation is that the cleaning time for extended stays is 10-12, 14-15 o'clock, why can't we be sure if there are guests cleaning again? 

About the housekeeper: To be honest, when I give feedback, I can solve the problem immediately, but I really have no customer service awareness! For example, when I gave feedback that the cleaning service woke up my child, the reply I typed in the chat was - Too pitiful baby? ? Well, maybe I think I am easy to talk to?
He came with a bubble machine and apologized to us, but where was the apology? When interacting with my child, he actually asked my child to apologize to me? ! What's going on? ! I almost swore on the spot. What did my child do wrong? Apologize to me? Isn't it the problem of your hotel that caused us to have a bad rest? ! Where did my child go wrong? ! So I refused to use other room fee reductions as an apology from the hotel, just want everyone to judge! I don't want to take benefits and give good reviews! Because the message I received is: just bear with it, if you are easy to talk to, the guests can be dealt with casually!
I am convinced! If you have no experience in customer service, I really suggest that your hotel train all service staff well. It's a waste of such a unique place...

About indoor parent-child service: It was raining on the first day, and everyone was in the hotel. The indoor playground was too small, unmanaged, too hot and messy. There were too many people in the parent-child organization activity area, which was also hot, without service, and messy. The emergency management ability was extremely low, and there were actually no activities in the hotel during the New Year's Day. It was a waste of such a good place.

About the mountain climbing loop service: I didn't make an appoin**ent for a car when I went out to climb the mountain. When I returned 1 kilometer, because the child couldn't walk and there were indeed a lot of items, I saw a speeding car and staff and asked if I could take it back. The answer was: This is our internal, and then there was no more. Haha, if it was two adults, there was no need to ask if they could take it back. The key is that there are children, even so, it is not allowed. Well, it is recommended that children with babies either take the car directly when they set off, or don't go hiking if they are too young. If you don't climb the mountain, there is nothing to play nearby, so it is recommended not to go.

3. Catering
About the buffet breakfast: It is very average, with few varieties and average taste.

About the buffet dinner: the variety is OK, and you can eat enough. If it is proportional to the price, forget it. It is not friendly to small children. For example, there is no porridge, no light food, except for soup noodles. The food is either spicy, some iced seafood, or fried. There is no scoop net in the self-service pot. In short, in short, it is not recommended to go! This is the first time I‚Äôve seen such a long review since I started traveling. I really can‚Äôt stand it!
